     1→/**
     2→ * XML Parser Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides XML parsing functionality using browser's native DOMParser API.
     5→ * Zero dependencies approach for fast, simple XML parsing (DECISIONS.md Decision 6).
     6→ */
     7→
     8→// TypeScript interfaces matching the XML schema from docs/sample/cover-letter.xml
     9→
    10→export interface Address {
    11→  street: string
    12→  city: string
    13→  state: string
    14→  zipCode: string
    15→}
    16→
    17→export interface ContactInformation {
    18→  phone: string
    19→  email: string
    20→}
    21→
    22→export interface Applicant {
    23→  name: string
    24→  address: Address
    25→  contactInformation: ContactInformation
    26→}
    27→
    28→export interface Achievement {
    29→  text: string
    30→}
    31→
    32→export interface Experience {
    33→  employer: string
    34→  achievements: Achievement[]
    35→}
    36→
    37→export interface Letter {
    38→  salutation: string
    39→  introduction: string
    40→  experienceSection: Experience[]
    41→  motivation: string
    42→  closing: string
    43→  signature: string
    44→}
    45→
    46→export interface Recipient {
    47→  position: string
    48→  company: string
    49→  address: Address
    50→}
    51→
    52→export interface ParsedData {
    53→  formatStyle?: string
    54→  applicant: Applicant
    55→  date: string
    56→  recipient: Recipient
    57→  letter: Letter
    58→}
    59→
    60→export interface ValidationResult {
    61→  isValid: boolean
    62→  error?: string
    63→}
    64→
    65→export interface ParseResult {
    66→  success: boolean
    67→  data?: ParsedData
    68→  error?: string
    69→}
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Helper function to safely extract text content from an XML element
    73→ */
    74→function getTextContent(element: Element | null, tagName: string, parentName: string = 'document'): string {
    75→  if (!element) {
    76→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    77→  }
    78→  const node = element.querySelector(tagName)
    79→  if (!node) {
    80→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    81→  }
    82→  return node.textContent?.trim() || ''
    83→}
    84→
    85→/**
    86→ * Parse address element (reusable for applicant and recipient addresses)
    87→ */
    88→function parseAddress(addressElement: Element | null, context: string): Address {
    89→  if (!addressElement) {
    90→    throw new Error(`Missing address element in ${context}`)
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  return {
    94→    street: getTextContent(addressElement, 'street', `${context} address`),
    95→    city: getTextContent(addressElement, 'city', `${context} address`),
    96→    state: getTextContent(addressElement, 'state', `${context} address`),
    97→    zipCode: getTextContent(addressElement, 'zipCode', `${context} address`),
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→/**
   102→ * Validate XML for well-formedness and basic schema requirements
   103→ *
   104→ * @param xmlString - XML string to validate
   105→ * @returns ValidationResult with isValid flag and optional error message
   106→ */
   107→export function validateXml(xmlString: string): ValidationResult {
   108→  if (!xmlString || xmlString.trim() === '') {
   109→    return {
   110→      isValid: false,
   111→      error: 'XML input is empty. Please provide valid XML content.',
   112→    }
   113→  }
   114→
   115→  const parser = new DOMParser()
   116→  const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   117→
   118→  // Check for parser errors
   119→  const parserError = xmlDoc.querySelector('parsererror')
   120→  if (parserError) {
   121→    // Extract meaningful error message from parsererror element
   122→    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'
   123→
   124→    // Provide user-friendly error messages for common issues
   125→    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {
   126→      return {
   127→        isValid: false,
   128→        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',
   129→      }
   130→    }
   131→    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {
   132→      return {
   133→        isValid: false,
   134→        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',
   135→      }
   136→    }
   137→    if (errorText.includes('invalid character') || errorText.includes('not well-formed')) {
   138→      return {
   139→        isValid: false,
   140→        error: 'XML contains invalid characters or syntax. Please check for special characters that need to be escaped.',
   141→      }
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    return {
   145→      isValid: false,
   146→      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,
   147→    }
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  // Check for root element
   151→  const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   152→  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'applicationDocument') {
   153→    return {
   154→      isValid: false,
   155→      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <applicationDocument>.',
   156→    }
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  // Check for required top-level elements
   160→  const requiredElements = ['applicant', 'date', 'recipient', 'letter']
   161→  for (const elementName of requiredElements) {
   162→    if (!root.querySelector(elementName)) {
   163→      return {
   164→        isValid: false,
   165→        error: `Missing required element: <${elementName}>. All application documents must include applicant, date, recipient, and letter sections.`,
   166→      }
   167→    }
   168→  }
   169→
   170→  return { isValid: true }
   171→}
   172→
   173→/**
   174→ * Parse XML string into structured data object
   175→ *
   176→ * @param xmlString - XML string to parse
   177→ * @returns ParseResult with success flag, parsed data, or error message
   178→ */
   179→export function parseXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {
   180→  try {
   181→    // First validate the XML
   182→    const validation = validateXml(xmlString)
   183→    if (!validation.isValid) {
   184→      return {
   185→        success: false,
   186→        error: validation.error,
   187→      }
   188→    }
   189→
   190→    const parser = new DOMParser()
   191→    const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   192→    const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   193→
   194→    // Extract formatStyle attribute (optional)
   195→    const formatStyle = root.getAttribute('formatStyle') || undefined
   196→
   197→    // Parse applicant section
   198→    const applicantElement = root.querySelector('applicant')
   199→    if (!applicantElement) {
   200→      throw new Error('Missing required element: applicant')
   201→    }
   202→
   203→    const applicant: Applicant = {
   204→      name: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'name', 'applicant'),
   205→      address: parseAddress(applicantElement.querySelector('address'), 'applicant'),
   206→      contactInformation: {
   207→        phone: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation phone', 'applicant'),
   208→        email: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation email', 'applicant'),
   209→      },
   210→    }
   211→
   212→    // Parse date
   213→    const date = getTextContent(root, 'date')
   214→
   215→    // Parse recipient section
   216→    const recipientElement = root.querySelector('recipient')
   217→    if (!recipientElement) {
   218→      throw new Error('Missing required element: recipient')
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    const recipient: Recipient = {
   222→      position: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'position', 'recipient'),
   223→      company: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'company', 'recipient'),
   224→      address: parseAddress(recipientElement.querySelector('address'), 'recipient'),
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Parse letter section
   228→    const letterElement = root.querySelector('letter')
   229→    if (!letterElement) {
   230→      throw new Error('Missing required element: letter')
   231→    }
   232→
   233→    // Parse experiences
   234→    const experienceElements = letterElement.querySelectorAll('experienceSection experience')
   235→    const experiences: Experience[] = Array.from(experienceElements).map((expElement) => {
   236→      const employer = expElement.querySelector('employer')?.textContent?.trim() || ''
   237→      const achievementElements = expElement.querySelectorAll('achievements achievement')
   238→      const achievements: Achievement[] = Array.from(achievementElements).map(ach => ({
   239→        text: ach.textContent?.trim() || '',
   240→      }))
   241→
   242→      return {
   243→        employer,
   244→        achievements,
   245→      }
   246→    })
   247→
   248→    const letter: Letter = {
   249→      salutation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'salutation', 'letter'),
   250→      introduction: getTextContent(letterElement, 'introduction', 'letter'),
   251→      experienceSection: experiences,
   252→      motivation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'motivation', 'letter'),
   253→      closing: getTextContent(letterElement, 'closing', 'letter'),
   254→      signature: getTextContent(letterElement, 'signature', 'letter'),
   255→    }
   256→
   257→    const parsedData: ParsedData = {
   258→      formatStyle,
   259→      applicant,
   260→      date,
   261→      recipient,
   262→      letter,
   263→    }
   264→
   265→    return {
   266→      success: true,
   267→      data: parsedData,
   268→    }
   269→  }
   270→  catch (error) {
   271→    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'
   272→    return {
   273→      success: false,
   274→      error: `Failed to parse XML: ${errorMessage}`,
   275→    }
   276→  }
   277→}
   278→
   279→/**
   280→ * Composable function to use XML parser in Vue components
   281→ */
   282→export function useXmlParser() {
   283→  return {
   284→    parseXml,
   285→    validateXml,
   286→  }
   287→}

     1→/**
     2→ * Template System Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides reactive template selection and management for document rendering.
     5→ * Active template is shared across all components via useState and persisted
     6→ * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import { onMounted, computed } from 'vue'
    10→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    11→import CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'
    12→import CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'
    13→import CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'
    14→
    15→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_template'
    16→
    17→// Template metadata interface for future extensibility
    18→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    19→  name: string
    20→  displayName: string
    21→  description: string
    22→}
    23→
    24→// Template registry type
    25→export interface TemplateRegistry {
    26→  [key: string]: {
    27→    component: Component
    28→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    29→  }
    30→}
    31→
    32→/**
    33→ * Template Registry
    34→ *
    35→ * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.
    36→ * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.
    37→ */
    38→const templates: TemplateRegistry = {
    39→  modern: {
    40→    component: CoverLetterModern,
    41→    metadata: {
    42→      name: 'modern',
    43→      displayName: 'Modern',
    44→      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',
    45→    },
    46→  },
    47→  classic: {
    48→    component: CoverLetterClassic,
    49→    metadata: {
    50→      name: 'classic',
    51→      displayName: 'Classic',
    52→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    53→    },
    54→  },
    55→  minimal: {
    56→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    57→    metadata: {
    58→      name: 'minimal',
    59→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    60→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    61→    },
    62→  },
    63→}
    64→
    65→/**
    66→ * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.
    67→ *
    68→ * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.
    69→ * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).
    70→ *
    71→ * @returns Reactive template state and control functions
    72→ */
    73→export function useTemplate() {
    74→  // Shared reactive state — useState ensures all components see the same value
    75→  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')
    76→
    77→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)
    78→  onMounted(() => {
    79→    try {
    80→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
    81→      if (saved && templates[saved]) {
    82→        activeTemplate.value = saved
    83→      }
    84→    }
    85→    catch {
    86→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
    87→    }
    88→  })
    89→
    90→  /**
    91→   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.
    92→   */
    93→  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {
    94→    if (!templates[name]) {
    95→      console.warn(`Template "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)
    96→      return
    97→    }
    98→    activeTemplate.value = name
    99→    try {
   100→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
   101→    }
   102→    catch {
   103→      // Ignore storage errors
   104→    }
   105→  }
   106→
   107→  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */
   108→  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(
   109→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,
   110→  )
   111→
   112→  /** Metadata for the currently active template */
   113→  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(
   114→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,
   115→  )
   116→
   117→  /** Names of all registered templates */
   118→  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   119→    return Object.keys(templates)
   120→  }
   121→
   122→  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */
   123→  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   124→    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  return {
   128→    activeTemplate,
   129→    setActiveTemplate,
   130→    currentTemplate,
   131→    currentTemplateMetadata,
   132→    getAvailableTemplates,
   133→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   134→  }
   135→}

    44→    </div>

    60→          :xml-content="debouncedXmlContent"

    63→      </div>

    67→
    68→<script setup lang="ts">
    69→import { ref, watch, onMounted, onUnmounted } from 'vue'
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Main Application Page - MVP 6: Dual-Panel Integration
    73→ *
    74→ * Features:
    75→ * - Welcome screen on first load (no saved data in localStorage)
    76→ * - Dual-panel 50/50 layout (CSS Grid)
    77→ * - 300ms debounced real-time updates (per DECISIONS.md)
    78→ * - Persists XML content to localStorage
    79→ * - Minimum 1024px responsive design
    80→ */
    81→
    82→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_xml_content'
    83→
    84→// Set page metadata
    85→useHead({
    86→  title: 'OhMyDoc - XML to HTML Transformer',
    87→})
    88→
    89→// Welcome screen is shown when no saved data exists
    90→const showWelcome = ref(true)
    91→const isSampleLoading = ref(false)
    92→
    93→// Reactive state for XML content
    94→const xmlContent = ref('')
    95→const debouncedXmlContent = ref('')
    96→
    97→// Debounce timer ref
    98→let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
    99→
   100→/**
   101→ * Debounce watcher: Updates preview 300ms after user stops typing
   102→ * Per DECISIONS.md Decision 5: 300ms < 500ms threshold provides smooth UX
   103→ * without feeling laggy or causing excessive re-parsing
   104→ */
   105→watch(xmlContent, (newValue) => {
   106→  if (debounceTimer) {
   107→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   108→  }
   109→
   110→  debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   111→    debouncedXmlContent.value = newValue
   112→    // Persist to localStorage so returning users skip the welcome screen
   113→    try {
   114→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, newValue)
   115→    }
   116→    catch {
   117→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   118→    }
   119→  }, 300)
   120→})
   121→
   122→/**
   123→ * Fetch and apply the sample cover letter XML.
   124→ * Called by the "Start with a sample" button on the welcome screen.
   125→ */
   126→async function loadSample() {
   127→  isSampleLoading.value = true
   128→  try {
   129→    const response = await fetch('/samples/cover-letter.xml')
   130→    if (!response.ok) {
   131→      throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`)
   132→    }
   133→    const sampleXml = await response.text()
   134→    xmlContent.value = sampleXml
   135→    debouncedXmlContent.value = sampleXml
   136→    showWelcome.value = false
   137→  }
   138→  catch (error) {
   139→    console.error('Error loading sample XML:', error)
   140→    // Still dismiss welcome and show an empty editor rather than getting stuck
   141→    showWelcome.value = false
   142→  }
   143→  finally {
   144→    isSampleLoading.value = false
   145→  }
   146→}
   147→
   148→/**
   149→ * On mount: restore saved content from localStorage.
   150→ * If content exists, skip the welcome screen and load it directly.
   151→ */
   152→onMounted(() => {
   153→  try {
   154→    const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
   155→    if (saved) {
   156→      xmlContent.value = saved
   157→      debouncedXmlContent.value = saved
   158→      showWelcome.value = false
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→  catch {
   162→    // Ignore localStorage errors; welcome screen will show as default
   163→  }
   164→})
   165→
   166→/**
   167→ * Cleanup: Clear debounce timer on component unmount
   168→ */
   169→onUnmounted(() => {
   170→  if (debounceTimer) {
   171→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   172→  }
   173→})
   174→</script>
   175→
   176→<style scoped>
   177→/**
   178→ * Main app container - full viewport height
   179→ */
   180→.app-container {
   181→  display: flex;
   182→  flex-direction: column;
   183→  height: 100vh;
   184→  width: 100vw;
   185→  overflow: hidden;
   186→}
   187→
   188→/**
   189→ * Dual-panel layout using CSS Grid
   190→ * 50/50 split between editor (left) and preview (right)
   191→ * Minimum width: 1024px total (512px per panel)
   192→ */
   193→.dual-panel-layout {
   194→  display: grid;
   195→  grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr;
   196→  flex: 1;
   197→  min-height: 0;
   198→  gap: 0;

   201→  min-width: 1024px;
   202→}

   208→.editor-panel {

   226→  transition: background-color 0.15s ease;
   227→}
   228→
   229→/**
   230→ * Responsive design for smaller screens

   232→ */
   233→@media (max-width: 1024px) {
   234→  .dual-panel-layout {
   235→    grid-template-columns: 1fr;

## Summary

I've successfully explored the requested files in the ohmydoc-v2 project. Here's what I found:

### 1. **composables/useXmlParser.ts** (288 lines)
Complete XML parser using browser's native DOMParser API. Features:
- TypeScript interfaces for the entire XML schema (Address, Applicant, Letter, Recipient, etc.)
- `parseXml()` function that converts XML strings to structured ParsedData objects
- `validateXml()` function with detailed error messages for common XML issues
- Composite helper functions like `parseAddress()` for reusable parsing logic
- No external dependencies (pure browser API)

### 2. **composables/useTemplate.ts** (136 lines)
Reactive template management system:
- Registry of three templates: Modern, Classic, and Minimal
- Imports Vue components from `/templates/{modern,classic,minimal}/`
- `useState()` for shared reactive state across components
- localStorage persistence (key: `ohmydoc_template`)
- Functions: `setActiveTemplate()`, `getAvailableTemplates()`, `getAllTemplateMetadata()`

### 3. **composables/useExport.ts**
**STATUS: File does NOT exist.** Not yet implemented. This would be needed for MVP 7 (HTML export functionality).

Main application page (MVP 6 integration):
- Welcome screen shown on first load when localStorage is empty
- Dual-panel 50/50 CSS Grid layout (Editor left, Preview right)

    32→export interface Experience {
    33→  employer: string
    34→  achievements: Achievement[]
    35→}
    36→
    37→export interface Letter {
    38→  salutation: string
    39→  introduction: string
    40→  experienceSection: Experience[]
    41→  motivation: string
    42→  closing: string
    43→  signature: string
    44→}
    45→
    46→export interface Recipient {
    47→  position: string
    48→  company: string
    49→  address: Address
    50→}
    51→
    52→export interface ParsedData {
    53→  formatStyle?: string
    54→  applicant: Applicant
    55→  date: string
    56→  recipient: Recipient
    57→  letter: Letter
    58→}
    59→
    60→export interface ValidationResult {
    61→  isValid: boolean
    62→  error?: string
    63→}
    64→
    65→export interface ParseResult {
    66→  success: boolean
    67→  data?: ParsedData
    68→  error?: string
    69→}
    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Helper function to safely extract text content from an XML element
    73→ */
    74→function getTextContent(element: Element | null, tagName: string, parentName: string = 'document'): string {
    75→  if (!element) {
    76→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    77→  }
    78→  const node = element.querySelector(tagName)
    79→  if (!node) {
    80→    throw new Error(`Missing required element: ${tagName} in ${parentName}`)
    81→  }
    82→  return node.textContent?.trim() || ''
    83→}
    84→
    85→/**
    86→ * Parse address element (reusable for applicant and recipient addresses)
    87→ */
    88→function parseAddress(addressElement: Element | null, context: string): Address {
    89→  if (!addressElement) {
    90→    throw new Error(`Missing address element in ${context}`)
    91→  }
    92→
    93→  return {
    94→    street: getTextContent(addressElement, 'street', `${context} address`),
    95→    city: getTextContent(addressElement, 'city', `${context} address`),
    96→    state: getTextContent(addressElement, 'state', `${context} address`),
    97→    zipCode: getTextContent(addressElement, 'zipCode', `${context} address`),
    98→  }
    99→}
   100→
   101→/**
   102→ * Validate XML for well-formedness and basic schema requirements
   103→ *
   104→ * @param xmlString - XML string to validate
   105→ * @returns ValidationResult with isValid flag and optional error message
   106→ */
   107→export function validateXml(xmlString: string): ValidationResult {
   108→  if (!xmlString || xmlString.trim() === '') {
   109→    return {
   110→      isValid: false,
   111→      error: 'XML input is empty. Please provide valid XML content.',
   112→    }
   113→  }
   114→
   115→  const parser = new DOMParser()
   116→  const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   117→
   118→  // Check for parser errors
   119→  const parserError = xmlDoc.querySelector('parsererror')
   120→  if (parserError) {
   121→    // Extract meaningful error message from parsererror element
   122→    const errorText = parserError.textContent || 'Unknown XML parsing error'
   123→
   124→    // Provide user-friendly error messages for common issues
   125→    if (errorText.includes('unclosed tag') || errorText.includes('Opening and ending tag mismatch')) {
   126→      return {
   127→        isValid: false,
   128→        error: 'XML has unclosed or mismatched tags. Please check that all opening tags have corresponding closing tags.',
   129→      }
   130→    }
   131→    if (errorText.includes('Unexpected end of file') || errorText.includes('premature end of data')) {
   132→      return {
   133→        isValid: false,
   134→        error: 'XML is incomplete. The document appears to end unexpectedly.',
   135→      }
   136→    }
   137→    if (errorText.includes('invalid character') || errorText.includes('not well-formed')) {
   138→      return {
   139→        isValid: false,
   140→        error: 'XML contains invalid characters or syntax. Please check for special characters that need to be escaped.',
   141→      }
   142→    }
   143→
   144→    return {
   145→      isValid: false,
   146→      error: `XML parsing error: ${errorText}`,
   147→    }
   148→  }
   149→
   150→  // Check for root element
   151→  const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   152→  if (!root || root.tagName !== 'applicationDocument') {
   153→    return {
   154→      isValid: false,
   155→      error: 'Invalid XML structure. Root element must be <applicationDocument>.',
   156→    }
   157→  }
   158→
   159→  // Check for required top-level elements
   160→  const requiredElements = ['applicant', 'date', 'recipient', 'letter']
   161→  for (const elementName of requiredElements) {
   162→    if (!root.querySelector(elementName)) {
   163→      return {
   164→        isValid: false,
   165→        error: `Missing required element: <${elementName}>. All application documents must include applicant, date, recipient, and letter sections.`,
   166→      }
   167→    }
   168→  }
   169→
   170→  return { isValid: true }
   171→}
   172→
   173→/**
   174→ * Parse XML string into structured data object
   175→ *
   176→ * @param xmlString - XML string to parse
   177→ * @returns ParseResult with success flag, parsed data, or error message
   178→ */
   179→export function parseXml(xmlString: string): ParseResult {
   180→  try {
   181→    // First validate the XML
   182→    const validation = validateXml(xmlString)
   183→    if (!validation.isValid) {
   184→      return {
   185→        success: false,
   186→        error: validation.error,
   187→      }
   188→    }
   189→
   190→    const parser = new DOMParser()
   191→    const xmlDoc = parser.parseFromString(xmlString, 'text/xml')
   192→    const root = xmlDoc.documentElement
   193→
   194→    // Extract formatStyle attribute (optional)
   195→    const formatStyle = root.getAttribute('formatStyle') || undefined
   196→
   197→    // Parse applicant section
   198→    const applicantElement = root.querySelector('applicant')
   199→    if (!applicantElement) {
   200→      throw new Error('Missing required element: applicant')
   201→    }
   202→
   203→    const applicant: Applicant = {
   204→      name: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'name', 'applicant'),
   205→      address: parseAddress(applicantElement.querySelector('address'), 'applicant'),
   206→      contactInformation: {
   207→        phone: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation phone', 'applicant'),
   208→        email: getTextContent(applicantElement, 'contactInformation email', 'applicant'),
   209→      },
   210→    }
   211→
   212→    // Parse date
   213→    const date = getTextContent(root, 'date')
   214→
   215→    // Parse recipient section
   216→    const recipientElement = root.querySelector('recipient')
   217→    if (!recipientElement) {
   218→      throw new Error('Missing required element: recipient')
   219→    }
   220→
   221→    const recipient: Recipient = {
   222→      position: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'position', 'recipient'),
   223→      company: getTextContent(recipientElement, 'company', 'recipient'),
   224→      address: parseAddress(recipientElement.querySelector('address'), 'recipient'),
   225→    }
   226→
   227→    // Parse letter section
   228→    const letterElement = root.querySelector('letter')
   229→    if (!letterElement) {
   230→      throw new Error('Missing required element: letter')
   231→    }
   232→
   233→    // Parse experiences
   234→    const experienceElements = letterElement.querySelectorAll('experienceSection experience')
   235→    const experiences: Experience[] = Array.from(experienceElements).map((expElement) => {
   236→      const employer = expElement.querySelector('employer')?.textContent?.trim() || ''
   237→      const achievementElements = expElement.querySelectorAll('achievements achievement')
   238→      const achievements: Achievement[] = Array.from(achievementElements).map(ach => ({
   239→        text: ach.textContent?.trim() || '',
   240→      }))
   241→
   242→      return {
   243→        employer,
   244→        achievements,
   245→      }
   246→    })
   247→
   248→    const letter: Letter = {
   249→      salutation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'salutation', 'letter'),
   250→      introduction: getTextContent(letterElement, 'introduction', 'letter'),
   251→      experienceSection: experiences,
   252→      motivation: getTextContent(letterElement, 'motivation', 'letter'),
   253→      closing: getTextContent(letterElement, 'closing', 'letter'),
   254→      signature: getTextContent(letterElement, 'signature', 'letter'),
   255→    }
   256→
   257→    const parsedData: ParsedData = {
   258→      formatStyle,
   259→      applicant,
   260→      date,
   261→      recipient,
   262→      letter,
   263→    }
   264→
   265→    return {
   266→      success: true,
   267→      data: parsedData,
   268→    }
   269→  }
   270→  catch (error) {
   271→    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred during parsing'
   272→    return {
   273→      success: false,
   274→      error: `Failed to parse XML: ${errorMessage}`,
   275→    }
   276→  }
   277→}
   278→
   279→/**
   280→ * Composable function to use XML parser in Vue components
   281→ */
   282→export function useXmlParser() {
   283→  return {
   284→    parseXml,
   285→    validateXml,
   286→  }
   287→}

    52→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    53→    },
    54→  },
    55→  minimal: {
    56→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    57→    metadata: {
    58→      name: 'minimal',
    59→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    60→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    61→    },
    62→  },
    63→}
    64→
    65→/**
    66→ * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.
    67→ *
    68→ * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.
    69→ * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).
    70→ *
    71→ * @returns Reactive template state and control functions
    72→ */
    73→export function useTemplate() {
    74→  // Shared reactive state — useState ensures all components see the same value
    75→  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')
    76→
    77→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)
    78→  onMounted(() => {
    79→    try {
    80→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
    81→      if (saved && templates[saved]) {
    82→        activeTemplate.value = saved
    83→      }
    84→    }
    85→    catch {
    86→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
    87→    }
    88→  })
    89→
    90→  /**
    91→   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.
    92→   */
    93→  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {
    94→    if (!templates[name]) {
    95→      console.warn(`Template "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)
    96→      return
    97→    }
    98→    activeTemplate.value = name
    99→    try {
   100→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
   101→    }
   102→    catch {
   103→      // Ignore storage errors
   104→    }
   105→  }
   106→
   107→  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */
   108→  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(
   109→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,
   110→  )
   111→
   112→  /** Metadata for the currently active template */
   113→  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(
   114→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,
   115→  )
   116→
   117→  /** Names of all registered templates */
   118→  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   119→    return Object.keys(templates)
   120→  }
   121→
   122→  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */
   123→  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   124→    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  return {
   128→    activeTemplate,
   129→    setActiveTemplate,
   130→    currentTemplate,
   131→    currentTemplateMetadata,
   132→    getAvailableTemplates,
   133→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   134→  }
   135→}
   136→

    70→
    71→/**
    72→ * Main Application Page - MVP 6: Dual-Panel Integration
    73→ *
    74→ * Features:
    75→ * - Welcome screen on first load (no saved data in localStorage)
    76→ * - Dual-panel 50/50 layout (CSS Grid)
    77→ * - 300ms debounced real-time updates (per DECISIONS.md)
    78→ * - Persists XML content to localStorage
    79→ * - Minimum 1024px responsive design
    80→ */
    81→
    82→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_xml_content'
    83→
    84→// Set page metadata
    85→useHead({
    86→  title: 'OhMyDoc - XML to HTML Transformer',
    87→})
    88→
    89→// Welcome screen is shown when no saved data exists
    90→const showWelcome = ref(true)
    91→const isSampleLoading = ref(false)
    92→
    93→// Reactive state for XML content
    94→const xmlContent = ref('')
    95→const debouncedXmlContent = ref('')
    96→
    97→// Debounce timer ref
    98→let debounceTimer: ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null = null
    99→
   100→/**
   101→ * Debounce watcher: Updates preview 300ms after user stops typing
   102→ * Per DECISIONS.md Decision 5: 300ms < 500ms threshold provides smooth UX
   103→ * without feeling laggy or causing excessive re-parsing
   104→ */
   105→watch(xmlContent, (newValue) => {
   106→  if (debounceTimer) {
   107→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   108→  }
   109→
   110→  debounceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   111→    debouncedXmlContent.value = newValue
   112→    // Persist to localStorage so returning users skip the welcome screen
   113→    try {
   114→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, newValue)
   115→    }
   116→    catch {
   117→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
   118→    }
   119→  }, 300)
   120→})
   121→
   122→/**
   123→ * Fetch and apply the sample cover letter XML.
   124→ * Called by the "Start with a sample" button on the welcome screen.
   125→ */
   126→async function loadSample() {
   127→  isSampleLoading.value = true
   128→  try {
   129→    const response = await fetch('/samples/cover-letter.xml')
   130→    if (!response.ok) {
   131→      throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`)
   132→    }
   133→    const sampleXml = await response.text()
   134→    xmlContent.value = sampleXml
   135→    debouncedXmlContent.value = sampleXml
   136→    showWelcome.value = false
   137→  }
   138→  catch (error) {
   139→    console.error('Error loading sample XML:', error)
   140→    // Still dismiss welcome and show an empty editor rather than getting stuck
   141→    showWelcome.value = false
   142→  }
   143→  finally {
   144→    isSampleLoading.value = false
   145→  }
   146→}
   147→
   148→/**
   149→ * On mount: restore saved content from localStorage.
   150→ * If content exists, skip the welcome screen and load it directly.
   151→ */
   152→onMounted(() => {
   153→  try {
   154→    const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
   155→    if (saved) {
   156→      xmlContent.value = saved
   157→      debouncedXmlContent.value = saved
   158→      showWelcome.value = false
   159→    }
   160→  }
   161→  catch {
   162→    // Ignore localStorage errors; welcome screen will show as default
   163→  }
   164→})
   165→
   166→/**
   167→ * Cleanup: Clear debounce timer on component unmount
   168→ */
   169→onUnmounted(() => {
   170→  if (debounceTimer) {
   171→    clearTimeout(debounceTimer)
   172→  }
   173→})

    14→    <!-- Loading State -->

    17→    </div>
    18→
    19→    <!-- Preview Rendering with Zoom Transform -->
    20→    <div
    21→      v-else-if="parsedData && templateComponent"

    23→      :style="containerStyle"
    24→    >
    25→      <Transition name="template-fade" mode="out-in">
    26→        <component :is="templateComponent" :key="activeTemplate" :data="parsedData" />

    28→    </div>
    29→
    30→    <!-- Placeholder State (no data) -->

    33→    </div>
    34→  </div>
    35→</template>

    37→<script setup lang="ts">
    38→import { ref, computed, watch } from 'vue'
    39→import { useXmlParser } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
    40→import { useTemplate } from '~/composables/useTemplate'
    41→import type { ParsedData } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
    42→
    43→// Ensure this component only runs on the client side (DOMParser is browser-only)
    44→defineOptions({
    45→  name: 'PreviewPanel',
    46→})
    47→
    48→/**
    49→ * PreviewPanel Component
    50→ *
    51→ * Integration point combining XML parser (MVP 2) and template system (MVP 3).
    52→ * Provides real-time preview of XML content with error handling and zoom support.
    53→ *
    54→ * Props:
    55→ * - xmlContent: XML string to parse and render
    56→ * - zoom: Zoom level for scaling (default: 1, range: 0.75 - 1.5)
    57→ */
    58→
    59→interface Props {
    60→  xmlContent: string
    61→  zoom?: number
    62→}
    63→
    64→const props = withDefaults(defineProps<Props>(), {
    65→  zoom: 1,
    66→})
    67→
    68→// Reactive state
    69→const parsedData = ref<ParsedData | undefined>(undefined)
    70→const error = ref<string | undefined>(undefined)
    71→const isLoading = ref(false)
    72→
    73→// Get composables
    74→const { parseXml } = useXmlParser()
    75→const { currentTemplate: templateComponent, activeTemplate } = useTemplate()
    76→
    77→// Computed style for zoom transform
    78→const containerStyle = computed(() => ({
    79→  transform: `scale(${props.zoom})`,
    80→  transformOrigin: 'top left',
    81→}))
    82→
    83→/**
    84→ * Parse XML and update component state
    85→ * Handles all parsing errors gracefully with user-friendly messages
    86→ */
    87→function updatePreview() {
    88→  isLoading.value = true
    89→  error.value = undefined
    90→  parsedData.value = undefined
    91→
    92→  try {
    93→    const result = parseXml(props.xmlContent)
    94→
    95→    if (result.success && result.data) {
    96→      parsedData.value = result.data
    97→      error.value = undefined
    98→    }
    99→    else {
   100→      error.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
   101→      parsedData.value = undefined
   102→    }
   103→  }
   104→  catch (err) {
   105→    const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
   106→    error.value = `Preview error: ${errorMessage}`
   107→    parsedData.value = undefined
   108→  }
   109→  finally {
   110→    isLoading.value = false
   111→  }
   112→}
   113→
   114→// Re-parse when xmlContent changes, and re-render when active template changes
   115→watch(
   116→  [() => props.xmlContent, activeTemplate],
   117→  () => {
   118→    updatePreview()
   119→  },
   120→  { immediate: true },
   121→)
   122→</script>

I need to create a document type registry system that abstracts away the cover-letter specificity, allowing each document type to define its own parser, templates, sample data, and metadata in one place. The key is to build `useDocumentType.ts` as a central registry where each document type declares its name, display name, sample XML path, parser function, available templates, and default template. Then I'll refactor `useXmlParser.ts` to keep the cover letter logic but make it reusable, and update all the components to reference document types through this registry instead of hardcoding cover-letter assumptions. Defining the document type interface... The core issue is that templates expect typed data, but different document types will have different shapes. For now, the pragmatic solution is to rename `ParsedData` to `CoverLetterData` while maintaining a backward-compatible export, since we're not adding new document types in this refactor. Actually, I should reconsider—the safest approach is keeping `ParsedData` as the cover letter's data type and letting each document type in the registry manage its own parser and data shape. Templates are inherently document-type-specific anyway, so a cover letter template renders `CoverLetterData` while a resume template would render `ResumeData`. The `PreviewPanel` just needs to work with whatever data the active document type's parser returns, rather than importing `ParsedData` directly. For the implementation, I'll keep it minimal since we're not adding new document types yet: create a `useDocumentType` hook to register cover letter as a document type and manage the active selection, update `useTemplate` to filter templates by document type, and keep `ParsedData` as-is for now with an optional alias rename.    134→
   135→<script setup lang="ts">
   136→import type { ParsedData } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'
   137→
   138→// Debug page for XML Parser (MVP 2)
   139→// This page demonstrates the useXmlParser composable in isolation
   140→
   141→useHead({
   142→  title: 'XML Parser Demo - OhMyDoc',
   143→})
   144→
   145→const { parseXml } = useXmlParser()
   146→
   147→// Reactive state
   148→const xmlInput = ref('')
   149→const parsedData = ref<ParsedData | null>(null)
   150→const validationError = ref<string | null>(null)
   151→const parseSuccess = ref(false)
   152→const isLoading = ref(false)
   153→
   154→// Format JSON for display with proper indentation
   155→const formattedJson = computed(() => {
   156→  if (!parsedData.value) return ''
   157→  return JSON.stringify(parsedData.value, null, 2)
   158→})
   159→
   160→// Load sample XML from /public/samples/cover-letter.xml
   161→async function loadSample() {
   162→  isLoading.value = true
   163→  validationError.value = null
   164→  parseSuccess.value = false
   165→
   166→  try {
   167→    const response = await fetch('/samples/cover-letter.xml')
   168→
   169→    if (!response.ok) {
   170→      throw new Error(`Failed to load sample: ${response.status} ${response.statusText}`)
   171→    }
   172→
   173→    const xmlContent = await response.text()
   174→    xmlInput.value = xmlContent
   175→
   176→    // Automatically parse the loaded sample
   177→    handleParse()
   178→  }
   179→  catch (error) {
   180→    const errorMessage = error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error occurred'
   181→    validationError.value = `Failed to load sample XML: ${errorMessage}`
   182→  }
   183→  finally {
   184→    isLoading.value = false
   185→  }
   186→}
   187→
   188→// Clear input and reset state
   189→function clearInput() {
   190→  xmlInput.value = ''
   191→  parsedData.value = null
   192→  validationError.value = null
   193→  parseSuccess.value = false
   194→}
   195→
   196→// Handle parse button click
   197→function handleParse() {
   198→  validationError.value = null
   199→  parseSuccess.value = false
   200→  parsedData.value = null
   201→
   202→  if (!xmlInput.value.trim()) {
   203→    validationError.value = 'Please provide XML content to parse'
   204→    return
   205→  }
   206→
   207→  const result = parseXml(xmlInput.value)
   208→
   209→  if (result.success && result.data) {
   210→    parsedData.value = result.data
   211→    parseSuccess.value = true
   212→  }
   213→  else {
   214→    validationError.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
   215→  }
   216→}
   217→
   218→// Load sample XML on component mount
   219→onMounted(() => {
   220→  loadSample()
   221→})
   222→</script>
   223→

  "file_path": "/home/gem/project/composables/useDocumentType.ts",
  "content": "/**\n * Document Type Registry Composable\n *\n * Manages the registry of supported document types and the currently active\n * document type. Each document type bundles its own parser, validator,\n * available templates, and sample XML path.\n *\n * Architecture note: this composable is the single source of truth for\n * \"what document type am I editing right now?\" All other composables and\n * components that need type-specific behaviour should consult it.\n */\n\nimport { computed, onMounted } from 'vue'\nimport { parseXml as parseCoverLetterXml, validateXml as validateCoverLetterXml } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'\nimport type { ValidationResult, ParseResult } from '~/composables/useXmlParser'\n\nconst LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_document_type'\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Public interfaces \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\nexport interface DocumentTypeConfig {\n  /** Internal key used in URLs, localStorage, and template associations */\n  name: string\n  /** Human-readable label shown in the UI */\n  displayName: string\n  /** Short description of the document type */\n  description: string\n  /** Path to the bundled sample XML (relative to /public) */\n  sampleXmlPath: string\n  /** Template to activate when this document type is first selected */\n  defaultTemplate: string\n  /** Names of templates registered in useTemplate that support this type */\n  templates: string[]\n  /** Parse an XML string into a typed data object for template rendering */\n  parse: (xmlString: string) => ParseResult\n  /** Validate well-formedness and schema requirements without full parsing */\n  validate: (xmlString: string) => ValidationResult\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Registry \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * All registered document types.\n *\n * To add a new type, append an entry here following the same shape as\n * 'cover-letter'. The parser and validator functions live in their own\n * composable (e.g. useResumParser.ts) and are imported at the top of this file.\n */\nconst documentTypes: Record<string, DocumentTypeConfig> = {\n  'cover-letter': {\n    name: 'cover-letter',\n    displayName: 'Cover Letter',\n    description: 'Professional cover letter for job applications',\n    sampleXmlPath: '/samples/cover-letter.xml',\n    defaultTemplate: 'modern',\n    templates: ['modern', 'classic', 'minimal'],\n    parse: parseCoverLetterXml,\n    validate: validateCoverLetterXml,\n  },\n}\n\n// \u2500\u2500\u2500 Composable \u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\u2500\n\n/**\n * Reactive document type selection.\n *\n * State is shared across all component instances via useState and persisted\n * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.\n */\nexport function useDocumentType() {\n  const activeDocumentType = useState<string>('activeDocumentType', () => 'cover-letter')\n\n  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only)\n  onMounted(() => {\n    try {\n      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)\n      if (saved && documentTypes[saved]) {\n        activeDocumentType.value = saved\n      }\n    }\n    catch {\n      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)\n    }\n  })\n\n  /**\n   * Switch to a different document type and persist the choice to localStorage.\n   * Also resets the active template to that type's default.\n   */\n  function setActiveDocumentType(name: string) {\n    if (!documentTypes[name]) {\n      console.warn(`Document type \"${name}\" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(documentTypes).join(', ')}`)\n      return\n    }\n    activeDocumentType.value = name\n    try {\n      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)\n    }\n    catch {\n      // Ignore storage errors\n    }\n  }\n\n  /** Config object for the currently active document type */\n  const currentDocumentType = computed<DocumentTypeConfig | undefined>(\n    () => documentTypes[activeDocumentType.value],\n  )\n\n  /** All registered document type config objects */\n  function getAvailableDocumentTypes(): DocumentTypeConfig[] {\n    return Object.values(documentTypes)\n  }\n\n  return {\n    activeDocumentType,\n    currentDocumentType,\n    setActiveDocumentType,\n    getAvailableDocumentTypes,\n  }\n}\n"

USERMESSAGE #110
✓ TOOL RESULT
SUCCESS 
     1→/**
     2→ * Template System Composable
     3→ *
     4→ * Provides reactive template selection and management for document rendering.
     5→ * Active template is shared across all components via useState and persisted
     6→ * to localStorage so the selection survives page reloads.
     7→ */
     8→
     9→import { onMounted, computed } from 'vue'
    10→import type { Component } from 'vue'
    11→import CoverLetterModern from '~/templates/modern/CoverLetterModern.vue'
    12→import CoverLetterClassic from '~/templates/classic/CoverLetterClassic.vue'
    13→import CoverLetterMinimal from '~/templates/minimal/CoverLetterMinimal.vue'
    14→
    15→const LS_KEY = 'ohmydoc_template'
    16→
    17→// Template metadata interface
    18→export interface TemplateMetadata {
    19→  name: string
    20→  displayName: string
    21→  description: string
    22→  /** Document type names this template supports (matches DocumentTypeConfig.name) */
    23→  documentTypes: string[]
    24→}
    25→
    26→// Template registry type
    27→export interface TemplateRegistry {
    28→  [key: string]: {
    29→    component: Component
    30→    metadata: TemplateMetadata
    31→  }
    32→}
    33→
    34→/**
    35→ * Template Registry
    36→ *
    37→ * Maps template names to their Vue components and metadata.
    38→ * All templates use the same ParsedData props interface for consistency.
    39→ */
    40→const templates: TemplateRegistry = {
    41→  modern: {
    42→    component: CoverLetterModern,
    43→    metadata: {
    44→      name: 'modern',
    45→      displayName: 'Modern',
    46→      description: 'Professional cover letter template with modern styling and clean typography',
    47→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    48→    },
    49→  },
    50→  classic: {
    51→    component: CoverLetterClassic,
    52→    metadata: {
    53→      name: 'classic',
    54→      displayName: 'Classic',
    55→      description: 'Traditional cover letter with table-based layout and formal styling',
    56→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    57→    },
    58→  },
    59→  minimal: {
    60→    component: CoverLetterMinimal,
    61→    metadata: {
    62→      name: 'minimal',
    63→      displayName: 'Minimal',
    64→      description: 'Clean, minimalist cover letter design with simple structure and generous whitespace',
    65→      documentTypes: ['cover-letter'],
    66→    },
    67→  },
    68→}
    69→
    70→/**
    71→ * Composable function to use the reactive template system in Vue components.
    72→ *
    73→ * Active template state is shared across all component instances via useState.
    74→ * On mount, the saved localStorage value is restored (client-side only).
    75→ *
    76→ * @returns Reactive template state and control functions
    77→ */
    78→export function useTemplate() {
    79→  // Shared reactive state — useState ensures all components see the same value
    80→  const activeTemplate = useState<string>('activeTemplate', () => 'modern')
    81→
    82→  // Restore from localStorage after hydration (client-only, runs once per component mount)
    83→  onMounted(() => {
    84→    try {
    85→      const saved = localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY)
    86→      if (saved && templates[saved]) {
    87→        activeTemplate.value = saved
    88→      }
    89→    }
    90→    catch {
    91→      // Ignore storage errors (private browsing, quota exceeded, etc.)
    92→    }
    93→  })
    94→
    95→  /**
    96→   * Switch to a different template and persist the choice to localStorage.
    97→   */
    98→  function setActiveTemplate(name: string) {
    99→    if (!templates[name]) {
   100→      console.warn(`Template "${name}" not found. Available: ${Object.keys(templates).join(', ')}`)
   101→      return
   102→    }
   103→    activeTemplate.value = name
   104→    try {
   105→      localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, name)
   106→    }
   107→    catch {
   108→      // Ignore storage errors
   109→    }
   110→  }
   111→
   112→  /** Reactive component for the currently active template */
   113→  const currentTemplate = computed<Component | undefined>(
   114→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.component,
   115→  )
   116→
   117→  /** Metadata for the currently active template */
   118→  const currentTemplateMetadata = computed<TemplateMetadata | undefined>(
   119→    () => templates[activeTemplate.value]?.metadata,
   120→  )
   121→
   122→  /** Names of all registered templates */
   123→  function getAvailableTemplates(): string[] {
   124→    return Object.keys(templates)
   125→  }
   126→
   127→  /** Metadata objects for all registered templates */
   128→  function getAllTemplateMetadata(): TemplateMetadata[] {
   129→    return Object.values(templates).map(t => t.metadata)
   130→  }
   131→
   132→  /** Metadata objects for templates that support the given document type */
   133→  function getTemplatesForDocumentType(docType: string): TemplateMetadata[] {
   134→    return Object.values(templates)
   135→      .filter(t => t.metadata.documentTypes.includes(docType))
   136→      .map(t => t.metadata)
   137→  }
   138→
   139→  return {
   140→    activeTemplate,
   141→    setActiveTemplate,
   142→    currentTemplate,
   143→    currentTemplateMetadata,
   144→    getAvailableTemplates,
   145→    getAllTemplateMetadata,
   146→    getTemplatesForDocumentType,
   147→  }
   148→}
   149→

    52→ * Provides real-time preview of XML content with error handling and zoom support.
    53→ *
    54→ * Props:

    56→ * - zoom: Zoom level for scaling (default: 1, range: 0.75 - 1.5)

    62→}

    97→      return
    98→    }
    99→

   101→
   102→    if (result.success && result.data) {
   103→      parsedData.value = result.data
   104→      error.value = undefined
   105→    }
   106→    else {
   107→      error.value = result.error || 'Unknown parsing error occurred'
   108→      parsedData.value = undefined
   109→    }
   110→  }

   113→    error.value = `Preview error: ${errorMessage}`
   114→    parsedData.value = undefined
   115→  }
   116→  finally {

   118→  }

The cover letter is the first (and currently only) registered type.\n- Adds `documentTypes: string[]` to `TemplateMetadata` in `useTemplate.ts` so templates declare which document types they support, plus a new `getTemplatesForDocumentType()` filter function.\n- Adds a **Document Type** dropdown to `AppHeader.vue` next to the existing Template dropdown; the Template dropdown now shows only templates compatible with the active document type.\n- `pages/index.vue` now loads the active document type's sample XML (rather than a hardcoded path); switching document types auto-loads the new sample.\n- `PreviewPanel.vue` dispatches to `currentDocumentType.parse()` instead of calling `parseXml()` directly, completing the abstraction.\n\n## What did NOT change\n\n- Cover letter functionality is identical \u2014 same parser, same three templates, same sample XML.\n- `useXmlParser.ts` and all template components are untouched.\n- Debug pages (`/debug/parser`, `/debug/template`, etc.) are untouched.\n\n## Test plan\n\n- [ ] App loads as before; cover letter sample renders correctly in all three templates\n- [ ] Template dropdown still switches templates\n- [ ] Document Type dropdown shows \"Cover Letter\" and selecting it reloads the sample XML\n- [ ] No TypeScript errors (`npm run build` passes)\n- [ ] `/debug/template` and `/debug/parser` pages still work correctly\n\n\ud83e\udd16 Generated with [Claude Code](https://claude.com/claude-code)\nEOF\n)\"",

ASSISTANTMESSAGE #127
## Status DONE ## What Changed - **`composables/useDocumentType.ts`** (new) — Document type registry with `DocumentTypeConfig` interface; cover letter registered with its parser, validator, sample path, and template list; exposes reactive `activeDocumentType`, `currentDocumentType`, `setActiveDocumentType`, `getAvailableDocumentTypes` - **`composables/useTemplate.ts`** — Added `documentTypes: string[]` to `TemplateMetadata`; tagged all three templates as `['cover-letter']`; added `getTemplatesForDocumentType(docType)` filter function - **`components/AppHeader.vue`** — Added Document Type dropdown alongside the existing Template dropdown; Template dropdown now filters reactively via `getTemplatesForDocumentType(activeDocumentType)` - **`pages/index.vue`** — `loadSample()` reads sample path from `currentDocumentType.sampleXmlPath`; added `watch(activeDocumentType)` to auto-load the new sample when the user switches document types - **`components/PreviewPanel.vue`** — Replaced direct `useXmlParser` import with `currentDocumentType.parse()` dispatch; watch now also triggers on `activeDocumentType` change ## Key Decisions - **`useDocumentType` doesn't depend on `useTemplate`** (and vice versa) — `AppHeader` wires them together, keeping each composable single-responsibility - **`ParsedData` type unchanged** — only one doc type exists today, so `PreviewPanel`'s ref stays typed as `ParsedData`; this will be revisited when a second type ships - **`{ immediate: false }` on the doc-type watch** in `index.vue` — prevents the localStorage-restore in `useDocumentType.onMounted` from triggering a redundant sample fetch on initial page load ## PR / Branch - Branch: `feat/document-type-abstraction` - PR: https://github.com/kimwwk/ohmydoc-using-claude-code-agent/pull/24
